  <raw>China's SAIC Motor plans to list in Hong Kong when market stabilizes - report



BEIJING (XFN-ASIA) - SAIC Motor, China's second-largest carmaker, plans to raise up to 2 bln usd in an initial public offering as soon as the Hong Kong stock market stabilizes, the South China Morning Post reported, citing sources.

'Risk appetite is next to nothing in the market right now,' the Hong Kong paper quoted a source as saying.
The launch of the deal was 'a question of market timing' and would come in the second half, another source said.
The Hang Seng Index hit an almost six-year high of 17,301.79 points last month but has since fallen to close yesterday at 15,973.11 as investors worried about the prospect of further interest rate increases.
Despite the slump, the index is still 7.37 pct ahead this year although analysts and investors expect the volatility to continue until the summer.
SAIC expects to attract investors with plans to make luxury cars based on foreign models and competes directly against Nanjing Automobile Group in producing cars based on Rover models, the report said.
SAIC's Shanghai-listed subsidiary, Shanghai Automotive, has joint ventures with Volkswagen and General Motors Corp.
BOCI, Merrill Lynch, Morgan Stanley and Deutsche Bank are arranging the SAIC deal, the report said.
virginie.mangin@xinhuafinance.com
vm/mas</raw>
